\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{7761 \textcolor{comment}{! anti-\/top decay routine, taken from MCFM, see hep-\/ph:/1204.1513}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7762        \textcolor{keywordtype}{implicit none}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7763        \textcolor{keywordtype}{integer} :: k4,e4,bbar,em,nubar}
\DoxyCodeLine{7764        \textcolor{keywordtype}{complex(8)} :: za(:,:),zb(:,:),dkamp(1:2)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7765 \textcolor{keywordtype}{       real}(8) :: NWAFactor\_Top,NWAFactor\_W}
\DoxyCodeLine{7766        \textcolor{keywordtype}{complex(8)} :: WProp}
\DoxyCodeLine{7767 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7768    \textcolor{comment}{! if one flattens the top wrt to e, then amp(2) = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7769        dkamp(1) = -\/m\_top * zb(bbar,nubar)*za(em,k4)/zb(e4,k4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7770        dkamp(2) = -\/zb(bbar,nubar)*za(em,e4)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7771 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7772        nwafactor\_top = 1d0/dsqrt(2d0*ga\_top*m\_top)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7773        nwafactor\_w   = 1d0/dsqrt(2d0*ga\_w*m\_w)}
\DoxyCodeLine{7774        wprop = (0d0,-\/1d0)*nwafactor\_w}
\DoxyCodeLine{7775 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7776        dkamp = dkamp * wprop * nwafactor\_top * gwsq}
\DoxyCodeLine{7777 }
\DoxyCodeLine{7778 }
